{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","updatedTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","title":"A major Amazon Air contractor says it won't return a $400 million bailout despite requests from Congress and booming business","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/amazon-contractor-atlas-air-declines-return-400-million-bailout-clyburn-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f0498863f7370596b3fd92b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Atlas Air Boeing 747-8F\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Frey/picture alliance/Getty</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Atlas Air, one of the largest US cargo carriers, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/atlas-air-amazon-air-contractor-receives-coronavirus-bailout-2020-6\">received</a> $407 million in government stimulus funding this spring.&#160;</li>\n<li>But business at the Amazon contractor, like other logistics companies, boomed amid the pandemic.</li>\n<li>Rep. Jim Clyburn called on Atlas and its peers last month to return the CARES Act funding, half of which is not required to be repaid.&#160;</li>\n<li>Atlas executives say the company fully qualified for the money and that it's been spent on its intended purpose: payroll.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Atlas Air, a cargo airline which includes Amazon as a major customer and investor, has seen business boom during the COVID-19 pandemic.</p><p>Yet this spring, as passenger carriers saw revenues plunge amid travel bans and lockdown orders, the company received <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/atlas-air-amazon-air-contractor-receives-coronavirus-bailout-2020-6\">$407 million from the US' payroll support program.</a> It was the largest amount received by any cargo airline under March's economic stimulus passed by Congress, only behind major passenger carriers like Delta and United. Just under half — $199,831,979 — must be repaid.</p><p>Now, with <a href=\"https://www.globenewswire.com/news-release/2020/11/05/2121032/0/en/Atlas-Air-Worldwide-Reports-Third-Quarter-2020-Results.html\">revenue and profits</a> once again nearing record highs above pre-pandemic levels, Democratic Rep. Jim Clyburn says Atlas and other cargo operators should return the full amount of the government-provided aid: \"Congress intended for these taxpayer funds to save jobs, not to provide windfalls to thriving businesses,\" the South Carolina delegate wrote in a letter October 20.</p><p>Atlas executives disagree, saying earlier in November that the company was \"fully qualified\" for the funds, as laid forth by the Treasury Department.</p><p>\"We are not intending to return the funds,\" chief executive John Dietrich said, noting that it was not a need-based program. \"We responded accordingly and have been in full compliance, not only with the committee's request, but sharing the documents and so forth that they've asked for, and we'll continue to fully cooperate.\"</p><p><em><strong>Read more:&#160;</strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-vaccine-cargo-airline-logistics-winners-losers-2020-11?r=gr-sub\" data-analytics-position=\"1\" data-analytics-module=\"\">6 cargo airlines and freight operators poised to win big when Pfizer's coronavirus vaccine is ready to go</a></em></p><p>Atlas Air did not immediately respond to a request for comment.&#160;</p><p>Scott Treibitz, a representative for IAP Local 2750, the union representing many Atlas Air pilots, pointed to <a href=\"https://www.sec.gov/Archives/edgar/data/1135185/000120919120055287/xslF345X03/doc4.xml\">recent stock sales</a> by executives and questioned if the stock would be at such high levels if not for the government funding. The union has for years been attempting to re-negotiate a new contract with Atlas, but say the company has refused to come to the table.&#160;</p><p>To be sure, Atlas Air, like many of its passenger and cargo peers, was significantly impacted by the pandemic, with profits falling more than 85% in the first quarter of 2020. By the third quarter, which Atlas reported on November 5, however, profits returned to a record-high.&#160;</p><p>\"2020 certainly has been an unprecedented year,\" Dietrich said. \"We expect volumes and yields in the fourth quarter to be driven by continued e-commerce growth and year-end airfreight demand, coupled with the ongoing reduction of passenger belly capacity in the market.\"</p><div multimillion-dollar payday thanks to Airbnb's initial public offering.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Airbnb publicly revealed <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/airbnb-files-s1-public-ipo-paperwork-revenue-losses-covid-19-2020-11\">the documents for its IPO</a> on Monday, providing a glimpse into the company's financials. The home-sharing startup hopes to raise $3 billion with its IPO, which would give it a valuation of about $30 billion, <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/airbnb-ipo/update-1-airbnb-to-make-ipo-filing-public-next-week-despite-covid-19-surge-sources-idUSL1N2HR0ZY\">according to a Reuters report</a> from earlier this month.&nbsp;</p>\n<p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"http://businessinsider.com/airbnb-ceo-brian-chesky-pandemic-challenges-resiliency-ipo-interview-2020-9?r=ah-sub\">Airbnb's Brian Chesky says what it was like to watch his company's revenue plunge 80% in eight weeks and how he decided to go public anyway in exclusive interview</a></em></p>\n<p>An exit for Airbnb means its early investors stand to profit — including Bezos.</p>\n<p>The Amazon CEO invested in Airbnb in two rounds, according to PitchBook data: the startup's Series A and Series B in 2010 and 2011, respectively. He used his personal venture-capital firm, Bezos Expeditions, to invest. The rounds totaled $119 million in funding for Airbnb, with investment from Ashton Kutcher's A-Grade Investments, Sequoia Capital, Andreessen Horowitz, and Greylock Partners.</p>\n<p>It's not clear how much Bezos invested in the company at the time or whether he still owns all of his shares.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>A spokesperson for Bezos Expeditions did not immediately respond to Business Insider's request for comment on its Airbnb investment.</p>\n<p>While Bezos' payday will likely net him millions of dollars, it will hardly make a difference for the richest man, whose net worth tops <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/billionaires/profiles/jeffrey-p-bezos/?sref=BWbpWjRm\">over $184 billion</a>. The majority of Bezos' wealth stems from his shares in Amazon. Bezos owns about 11% of the e-commerce giant he founded in 1994, <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-11-04/amazon-ceo-bezos-sells-1-42-billion-of-shares?sref=BWbpWjRm\">according to Bloomberg</a>.</p>\n<p>Beyond his substantial Amazon stake, Bezos is a prolific investor, with early investments in Google, Uber, and Twitter. Bezos was also an early investor in Business Insider, though he has since sold his stake in the company.</p>\n<p><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Got a tip? 13:38:42","updatedTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","title":"Watch live: SpaceX's Crew Dragon spaceship is docking 4 astronauts to the International Space Station","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/watch-live-spacex-crew-dragon-docking-to-international-space-station-2020-11","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac5bbb98669500182b5820?format=jpeg\" alt=\"spacex nasa crew 1 mission 4x3\" height=\"1437\" width=\"1917\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying aboard SpaceX&#39;s Crew-1 mission for NASA are astronauts (from left) Mike Hopkins, Soichi Noguchi, Shannon Walker, and Victor Glover.\n<p class=\"copyright\">SpaceX; NASA; Samantha Lee/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>SpaceX just <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-launches-rocket-mission-nasa-astronauts-crew-1-dragon-spaceship-2020-11\">launched</a> four astronauts into orbit aboard its Crew Dragon spaceship.</li>\n<li>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/crew-1-astronaut-bios-spacex-nasa-mission-2020-11\">astronauts</a> are expected to dock to the International Space Station on Monday at 11 p.m. ET.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/nasa-astronauts-connect-spacex-crew-dragon-spaceship-international-space-station-2020-5\">Docking</a> is a complex series of maneuvers that must go right for the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-crew-1-mission-timeline-nasa-astronaut-launch-2020-11\">Crew-1 mission</a> to be successful.</li>\n<li>Watch this crucial part of the mission live on NASA TV's broadcast below.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p><strong data-stringify-type=\"bold\"><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">Update</em></strong><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">: The spaceship&#160;</em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astronauts-attach-spacex-crew-dragon-spaceship-international-space-station-2020-11\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-stringify-link=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astronauts-attach-spacex-crew-dragon-spaceship-international-space-station-2020-11\" data-sk=\"tooltip_parent\">docked with the International Space Station</a></em><em data-stringify-type=\"italic\">&#160;at 11:01 p.m. ET on Monday.</em></p><p>SpaceX rocketed four astronauts into Earth's orbit on Sunday, kicking off its most ambitious spaceflight yet for NASA.</p><p>The mission, called Crew-1, is set to bring Mike Hopkins, Victor Glover, and Shannon Walker of NASA, along with <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-starship-dearmoon-crew-japanese-astronaut-soichi-noguchi-yusaku-maezawa-2020-9\">Soichi Noguchi</a> of the Japanese Aerospace Exploration Agency, to the International Space Station. They're scheduled to stay there for six months, constituting the longest human spaceflight in NASA history.</p><p>The astronauts launched aboard a Crew Dragon spaceship on Sunday evening. Once in orbit, the crew changed out of their spacesuits into more comfortable clothes, ate dinner, and settled down for a night's rest.</p><p>All in all, they're set to spend 27 hours inside the Crew Dragon capsule, which the astronauts have <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/astronauts-name-spacex-spaceship-resilience-ahead-of-nasa-launch-2020-9\">named Resilience</a>, before the ship fully lines up with and docks to a port on the station. The docking operation requires a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-spaceship-docking-video-game-simulator-international-space-station-2020-5\">complex set of maneuvers</a>, and the Crew-1 launch won't be considered complete until it's done. If the spaceship can't dock, it may have to turn around, plummet through Earth's atmosphere, and parachute into the ocean so NASA and SpaceX can recover the astronauts.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f761fa80ab50d00184ada17?format=jpeg\" alt=\"crew dragon iss docking demo2 spacex\" height=\"1403\" width=\"1872\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Crew Dragon docks to the International Space Station, May 31, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://images.nasa.gov/details-iss063e021463\" target=\"_blank\">Chris Cassidy</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>If docking succeeds, though, Crew-1 will become the first operational mission to come out of a decade-long effort to restore NASA's human spaceflight capabilities. Through its <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-boeing-nasa-commercial-crew-program-launch-astronauts-2020-1\">Commercial Crew Program</a>, the space agency has funded the development of private, astronaut-ready launch systems from SpaceX and Boeing. NASA has spent more than $6 billion on the program, according to <a href=\"https://www.planetary.org/articles/nasas-commercial-crew-is-a-great-deal-for-the-agency\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"ab8c5da0f9f5016bcde3f0e916b5aa81\">The Planetary Society</a>.</p><p>SpaceX on Tuesday became the first company to receive NASA's human-spaceflight <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/nasa-certifies-spacex-fly-astronauts-crew-dragon-spaceship-2020-11\">certification</a> for a commercial system, and Crew-1 marks its first \"operational\" mission. The company proved its human-launch abilities this summer when it successfully rocketed NASA astronauts <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/nasa-astronauts-doug-hurley-bob-behnken-biography-spacex-demo2-2020-5\">Bob Behnken and Doug Hurley</a> to the ISS and back in a test flight called Demo-2.</p><p>Now, the four astronauts on the Resilience spaceship are awake and monitoring the docking operation.</p><p>\"We're not done yet,\" Kathy Lueders, NASA's head of human spaceflight, told reporters two hours after the launch. \"That spacecraft's out there with those four precious crew members on [it], and we're going to get them safely to the International Space Station tomorrow.\"</p><p>NASA TV is broadcasting live video of the docking on its stream below:</p><iframe width=\"560\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/21X5lGlDOfg\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe><p>NASA plans to continue broadcasting through about 2 a.m. ET, after the agency expects Crew-1 astronauts to float inside the ISS, greet each other, and wrap up a traditional docking ceremony.&#160;</p><h2>How a 13-ton spaceship precision maneuvers into an ISS port</h2><p>The flight is programmed to be automatic, but the crew will keep tabs on the process. If anything goes wrong, the astronauts can <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-spaceship-docking-video-game-simulator-international-space-station-2020-5\">manually control the spacecraft</a>.</p><p>\"They won't have to push any buttons or fire any thrusters, Dragon is doing this all on its own — it's completely autonomous,\" Leah Cheshier, a NASA communications specialist, said during NASA TV and SpaceX's joint broadcast on Monday night. \"The crew is just monitoring when you see them looking at their screens.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2aea7402d49001924f22c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"spacex crew dragon endeavour astronauts touch screen nasa astronauts bob behnken doug hurley\" height=\"1416\" width=\"1889\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>NASA astronauts Bob Behnken and Doug Hurley prepare to depart the International Space Station aboard SpaceX&#39;s Crew Dragon on August 1, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NASA</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Early in the docking process, Resilience stopped about 400 meters below the space station, later swing up and in front of the facility. The capsule then began a series of automated maneuvers to close in on the ISS. First, it began slowly pulling up to a point about 220 meters ahead of the station's Node 2 forward port.</p><p>Assuming all goes well, the spaceship's autopilot will continue inching it toward the football-field-size, orbiting laboratory and line up its docking system with the adapter on the port.</p><div class=\"insider-raw-embed\"><div style='position:relative; padding-bottom:calc(52.72% + 44px)'><iframe src='https://gfycat.com/ifr/QuerulousThickHamster' frameborder='0' scrolling='no' width='100%' height='100%' style='position:absolute;top:0;left:0;' allowfullscreen></iframe></div></div><p>Crew Dragon's automated and manual docking systems have both been tested. During Demo-2, Behnken and Hurley turned off the auto-pilot to and controlled the vehicle. Demo-2 was a test flight, after all, and part of it was making sure the backup systems worked.</p><p>\"It flew just about like the [simulator], so my congratulations to the folks in Hawthorne. It flew really well, very really crisp,\" Hurley said during <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-crew-dragon-international-space-station-docking-youtube-live-webcast-2020-5\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"2dfda7bf388fff0dc6d04aef77ed41a8\">a live webcast</a> after the docking, adding that its handling was \"a little sloppier\" in an up-down direction, though this was as expected.</p><p>If there are no issues, and the new Crew Dragon firmly secures itself to the ISS in the same way the last ship did, the station's adapter will slowly fill with air, allow the astronauts inside to open their hatches, and then greet each other with zero-gravity hugs.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5ed3f8baaee6a82eaa2760f3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"nasa astronauts bob behnken doug hurley crew dragon docking greeting international space station crew chris cassidy cosmonauts anatoly ivanishin ivan vagner iss may 31 2020\" height=\"446\" width=\"800\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>NASA astronauts Bob Behnken and Doug Hurley float into the International Space Station on May 31, 2020, after riding SpaceX&#39;s Crew Dragon to orbit.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=21X5lGlDOfg\" target=\"_blank\">NASA</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Kate Rubins, the NASA astronaut currently on the ISS, will be waiting to greet them.</p><p>\"I have some great friends flying on that vehicle, so I'm going to be pretty happy to open the hatch and welcome them to the space station,\" she told Business Insider.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f92dcbb212113001874062e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Nasa kate rubins voting astronaut\" height=\"1195\" width=\"1594\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>NASA Astronaut Kate Rubins.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NASA</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Russian cosmonauts Sergey Ryzhikov and Sergey Kud-Sverchkov will also welcome Crew-1 to the space station.</p><p>The Crew Dragon will remain attached to the ISS for the astronauts' entire stay there. The Resilience capsule has a new set of solar panels that are much more durable than the ones that flew with Behnken and Hurley. Those previous solar panels would have begun to degrade in the harsh radiation of space after just 110 days (that mission only lasted two months). Resilience, however, is certified to weather 210 days — nearly seven months — in space.</p><h2>This may not be the only docking in the Crew-1 mission</h2><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f2470fa24381733fd1a60e1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"spacex crew dragon endeavour docked international space station iss july 1 2020 iss063e034054\" height=\"3076\" width=\"4101\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>SpaceX&#39;s Crew Dragon &#34;Endeavour&#34; spaceship photographed by astronauts Bob Behnken and Chris Cassidy while performing a spacewalk on July 1, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.nasa.gov/image-feature/view-of-the-spacex-crew-dragon-and-japans-htv-9-resupply-ship-0\" target=\"_blank\">NASA</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>In another <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-6-major-upgrades-to-spaceship-rocket-for-nasa-astronauts-2020-11\">major upgrade</a>, Resilience is programmed with the ability to move itself to another of the four ports on the US section of the ISS, in order to make room for other incoming spaceships.</p><p>\"It's getting a little crowded in space. And that's a really good thing,\" NASA astronaut Suni Williams said in a Friday briefing.</p><p>Williams is set to fly on the first operational mission of Boeing's CST-100 Starliner — that company's spaceship for astronauts, which was funded and designed through NASA's Commercial Crew Program as well. The Starliner is set to reattempt an uncrewed test flight to the space station in 2021, since the first test failed. That might require the Crew Dragon to move to a different port.</p><p>To relocate the spaceship, the crew will climb back in and run new software that should maneuver the Crew Dragon away from its original docking point, the Forward Port, and re-dock to the station's Zenith Port.</p><p><em>This story has been updated. It was originally published at 6:24 p.m. ET on November 16, 2020.</em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 13:38:42","updatedTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","title":"Cofounder of accelerator Spark Labs attributes the success of Korean startups to global mindset","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/cofounder-of-accelerator-spark-labs-attributes-success-of-korean-startups-to-global-mindset-2020-11","description":"<div class=\"content-header\"><p><a href=\"https://businessinsider.com/tb/the-people-transforming-business-in-2020-9\"><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://media.tbistatic.com/bistudios/_00/dev/ING/story_banners/ING_edit_banner.png?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Transforming Business\" height=\"\" width=\"\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\"></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></a></p></div><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fadc0224652d40019744247?format=jpeg\" alt=\"JIMMY KIM   SparkLabs\" height=\"2501\" width=\"3335\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Jimmy Kim, Cofounder and partner of SparkLabs Global Ventures\n<p class=\"copyright\">Spark Labs</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>Korea's startup economy is growing fast, helped by the country's reputation for technological innovation</strong></li>\n<li><strong>Cofounded by Jimmy Kim, Spark Labs is a Seoul-based accelerator for Korean startups that want to go global</strong></li>\n<li><strong>Since its inception in 2012, Spark Labs has invested in over 170 companies and has raised over $600 million in follow-on funding</strong></li>\n<li><strong>Kim identifies B2B software services as a transformational investment space for Korean companies looking to grow overseas</strong></li>\n<li>Because of his work, Business Insider named Kim to our annual list of the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tb/the-list-of-300-people-transforming-business-in-asia-2020-9\">10 leaders transforming investing in Asia.</a></li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tb/the-people-transforming-business-in-2020-9\"><strong>Visit Business Insider's Transforming Business homepage for more stories</strong></a><strong>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p>From K-Pop to K-Drama and even an Oscar win for Best Film, Korea is doing an impressive job in terms of global soft power. And there is one other area where Korea is beginning to emerge globally against its Asian peers: the startup scene. Alongside the likes of Singapore, Shenzhen, Jakarta, and others, Seoul has established itself as a key startup hub in the region, nurturing numerous tech unicorns along the way.&#160;</p><p>This is not too surprising when set against the country's global reputation for technological innovation, thanks to the likes of Samsung, Hyundai, LG, and more. Indeed, the international success of these more established Korean conglomerates is a major factor driving the growth of Korea's startup economy, according to Jimmy Kim, cofounder of Korean accelerator Spark Labs.</p><p>\"The reason Korea has been so successful is because the mindset has been that we have to go global,\" he says. \"If you are doing well in Japan or in China, going global is not a priority, whereas in Korea the only way you are going to survive in any company right now is that you have to look overseas, because the population is not enough alone to support a unicorn or decacorn valuation.\"</p><h2><strong>Helping Korean firms succeed overseas</strong></h2><p>Spark Labs was founded in 2012 by Kim and cofounders Bernard Moon and John Hanjoo Lee. All three came from a startup background – reflecting one of the company's mantras of 'founded by entrepreneurs for entrepreneurs.' For Kim, this meant time spent as a founding investor in online gaming firm Studio Ex and as a co-founder of N3N, an IoT enterprise software company.</p><p>\"The key thing we found was that although Korean companies are very innovative and leaders in their field, startups have a hard time going abroad, seeking overseas markets,\" says Kim. \"The problem we found was that entrepreneurs in the early stage really have a hard time trying to scale up so Spark Labs was founded on this premise to help entrepreneurs go global.\"</p><p>Kim says the company looked at Y Combinator as its benchmark. \"There are three components to Y Combinator that we really liked. First of all, it was giving startups the cash that they need. Second was giving them mentorship and helping them reach the next milestone, to achieve follow-on funding. Thirdly was a demo day where people can showcase what they've done over the past three four months. Exposure was very important.\"</p><p>Spark Labs Global Accelerator Program has two batches a year, amounting to 20 companies a year, whittled down from an original 600 applicants. Kim and his fellow founders and company partners take a hands-on approach, steering the chosen startups through a 14-week process, ending in a Demo Day in front of potential new investors.</p><p>For Kim, the mentorship element during this process is crucial. \"We tell people that we can't show you how to succeed, but we can definitely tell you how to fail,\" he says. \"Mentorship is first of all being a soundboard. Helping entrepreneurs crystalize what that essence of the business is. Each company we attach them to on average five mentors who can give them insight. The whole essence of the mentorship is having someone to talk to and someone to bounce your ideas off.\"</p><p>Spark Labs has to-date completed 15 batches as part of the accelerator program. Kim says the company has invested in over 170 plus companies. Success for him though is linked less with immediate business success and more with raising additional funds, noting that 70% of companies going through the process received between $1 million and $2 million in follow-on funding after the demo day.</p><p>\"We're very happy with the fact that our companies have raised over $600 million in follow-on funding,\" he adds. \"The market cap of all the companies we have invested in is over $2 billion.\"&#160;</p><h2><strong>The will to go global</strong></h2><p>Kim says the company is not looking at specific startup categories when choosing entrepreneurs to back. \"A lot of people say are you e-commerce? Are you gaming? But we believe that the future is data, and when we look at companies we look if they are either generating data, accumulating data or analyzing data. Those are the lens we use right now, the pillars of Spark Labs.\"</p><p>In terms of companies with the potential to break global markets, Kim points to Spark Labs-funded beauty platform MBX (Memebox) who launched their Kaja brand in the US with Sephora.&#160; \"MBX is a Korean data-driven cosmetics company, they've raised about $190 million to date,\" says Kim.&#160; \"Kaja is going global right now. The whole thing of K-culture right now, K-Beauty is definitely a part of this. I think you'll see a stream of companies that will extend that boundary.\"&#160;</p><p>However, Kim sees the most transformational investment potential lying in B2B software and cloud services. \"COVID-19 has really brought the need for automation, not just factory automation but intra-company automation and solutions that make it easier to communicate and collaborate and contribute. It's not just about the big e-commerce B2C companies, the real investment is going to be in the software services space.\"</p><p>Ultimately though, Spark Labs are investing in people and in entrepreneurs.&#160; \"It's the will and desire and vision to go global,\" he says.</p><h2><strong>Government lending a hand</strong></h2><p>Spark Labs, of course, is not alone in supporting startup culture in Korea, and Kim points to the progress being made in the public sphere. \"The government is conscious [of the need to go global] and has been trying to support and spark entrepreneurship.\"</p><p>One example is TIPS (Accelerator Investment-Driven Tech Incubator Program for Startups). Startups under three years old can apply for the government program with selected companies eligible to receive up to more than $800,000 USD in funding, to be used as seed capital, research and development expenses or marketing fees. The program is benchmarked against a similar initiative in Israel.&#160;</p><p>\"Korea has realized that Series A funding is very high risk and they have to be able to provide a sandbox that allows people to fail. That's where I think Korea has been very aggressive and very successful.</p><p>Kim argues that this mix of VC and government funding combined with the growing entrepreneurial spirit in Korea is what is paying dividends. \"Korea is not as big as Japan or China or even Indonesia,\" he says. \"But because of that our export economy is strong and we are very fortunate to have companies like Samsung or LG or Hyundai. These companies, our precursors, were also startups a long time ago, so we have it in our DNA.\"</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 13:38:42","updatedTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","title":"How to use Skype on an iPad to call or chat with your contacts","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-skype-on-ipad","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e1cfe3e24fe1223875a1613?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Skype Logo app\" height=\"1999\" width=\"2999\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can use Skype on your iPad to communicate with others via messaging or video or audio calls.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas for iPad gives you more screen space, allowing you to keep Skype open while you navigate through other tabs.</li>\n<li>Here's how to use all the features of the Skype app on your iPad.</li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul><p><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/category/skype\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Skype</a> for iPad allows you to enjoy the video chat service in an app specifically designed for your Apple tablet.</p><p>Whether you're interviewing for a new job or keeping in touch with a friend overseas, the app is easy to use, and is essentially three main tabs: Chats, Calls, and Contacts.&#160;</p><p>Though the interface looks similar to Skype&#160;for iPhone, Skype&#160;for iPad allows for more screen room to do things like keep chats open while you browse.</p><p>Here's a quick guide to Skype for iPad.</p><h2><strong>How to use the Skype for </strong><strong>iPad</strong><strong> app</strong></h2><p><strong>1. </strong>Open the Skype app on your iPad. If you haven't already, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-download-apps-on-ipad-for-free\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">download the app</a> from the App Store and log into your Skype account.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e5fed27fee23d484260edc5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to Skype on iPad\" height=\"2048\" width=\"1536\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Download Skype for iPad.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marissa Perino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2. </strong>When you first log in, you'll be prompted to choose your theme. Continue clicking through the pop-ups with the blue \"Continue\" button. Other prompts will include syncing your contacts. All of these changes can be altered at a later time.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e5fed3efee23d445f1c70b2?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to Skype on iPad\" height=\"2048\" width=\"1536\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Set up Skype for iPad.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marissa Perino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3. </strong>Upon opening Skype for iPad, you'll find the three main tabs at the bottom of the screen: Chats, Calls, and Contacts.&#160;</p><p>The Skype app should automatically open to the Chats tab, where you'll see any recent chats appear.</p><ul><li>This is also where you'll find your notifications center.</li><li>You can also start a new message in this tab by tapping \"Type a message\" or searching for the contact.</li><li>You can also add Emojis, photos, or voice messages to your chat.</li></ul><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e5fed5dfee23d5437784024?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to Skype on iPad\" height=\"2048\" width=\"1536\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Chats page.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marissa Perino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Tap the Calls tab to see your recent calls or start a new video or phone call.</p><ul><li>You can start a new call by tapping the phone or camera icon next to the person's name or in the top right corner.</li><li>Any chats you have open will remain visible in the space on the right.</li><li>Once you start a call, you can tap the chat icon in the bottom left corner to open your chats.</li></ul><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e5fed7ffee23d5446737d3b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to Skype on iPad\" height=\"2048\" width=\"1536\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Calls page on the left, and a chat on the right.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marissa Perino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Finally, tap the Contacts tab to see a list of your contacts.</p><ul><li>Tap the icon of a person with a plus \"+\" sign at the top right of the Contacts window to add a new contact.</li><li>Search for particular contacts using the left hand search bar labeled \"People, groups &#38; messages.\"</li></ul><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5e5fed9ffee23d48a252c737?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to Skype on iPad\" height=\"2048\" width=\"1536\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Your Contacts page.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Marissa Perino/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><div id=\"ProductCard_5cf009db11e205572467a993\" style=\"position:relative; display:block; width: any active memberships.</li>\n<li>After submitting a request for account deletion, you have 14 days to stop the process.</li>\n<li>It can take up to 30 days to fully delete a Patreon account.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Whether you're a patron or a creator on Patreon, deleting your account is a fairly straightforward process — but it takes some time. To delete your Patreon account, you must submit your account for deletion through Patreon's privacy center, and it can take up to 30 days to process your request.</p><p>Here's how it's done.</p><h2>How to delete your Patreon account and data</h2><p><strong>1.</strong> Go to <a href=\"https://privacy.patreon.com/#patreon-profile-information\">Patreon's privacy policy center</a>, then click the \"Take Control\" button.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d2641c741f0019aca123?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 1\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can delete your Patreon account by going to the site&#39;s Privacy portal.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2.</strong> Click \"Erase.\" If promoted, log into your Patreon account at this time.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d2ac402d49001924f354?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 2\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Choose Erase if you want your data scrubbed by Patreon.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> Click \"Allow\" to give Transcend, Patreon's data deletion partner, access to your account in order to erase it.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d31b402d49001924f358?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 3\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You must allow Transcend to delete your relevant data.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> Click \"Confirm Request.\" <a href=\"https://support.patreon.com/hc/en-us/articles/204605915-Delete-my-Patreon-account\">Patreon notes</a> that this process of erasing your account and data will take up to 30 days, and you have 14 days to stop the process via follow-up emails which allow you to cancel the data deletion. Transcend will send email updates on the status of deletion requests.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d33e1c741f0019aca12a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete your Patreon 4\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You will have 14 days to undo your confirmed account deletion.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>How to cancel active Patreon memberships</h2><p><a href=\"https://support.patreon.com/hc/en-us/articles/204605915-Delete-my-Patreon-account\">The Patreon help page</a> notes that while deleting your account erases your data from the platform, it is not a replacement for canceling active memberships or pending payments on your account. If your goal is to simply <a href=\"https://support.patreon.com/hc/en-us/articles/360005502572\">delete active memberships</a> for creators you're a patron of, you can do so while still keeping your account.</p><p><strong>1.</strong> On a desktop, hover over your profile icon on the top right of the screen, then click \"Manage memberships.\"</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d4a71c741f0019aca132?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 5\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Select manage memberships from your Patreon settings menu.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>2.</strong> Navigate to the \"Active Memberships\" tab, then click \"Edit\" on any memberships you wish to cancel future payments for.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d4cb402d49001924f361?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 6\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Active Memberships tab should be the default window.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>3.</strong> Click \"Edit or Cancel Membership,\" located underneath the \"Update\" button.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d4f41c741f0019aca133?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 7\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The option to cancel your membership is just beneath the Update button.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p><strong>4.</strong> Select \"Cancel your membership,\" then click the \"Cancel your membership\" button to confirm this action.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb2d52f402d49001924f363?format=jpeg\" alt=\"How to delete Patreon 8\" height=\"1800\" width=\"2880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You will need to confirm your account deletion twice.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abigail Abesamis Demarest/Business astronaut crew gave a video tour of the Crew Dragon spaceship from orbit on Monday.</li>\n<li>They also gave pilot Victor Glover a gold pin to commemorate his first spaceflight.</li>\n<li>Watch the after SpaceX rocketed four astronauts into orbit, the crew gave a video tour of their Crew Dragon spaceship.</p><p>NASA astronauts Mike Hopkins, Victor Glover and Shannon Walker, and Japanese Aerospace Agency astronaut <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-starship-dearmoon-crew-japanese-astronaut-soichi-noguchi-yusaku-maezawa-2020-9\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"719a6ad784c8e5fdb64239404c8e1ee0\">Soichi Noguchi</a> lifted off from NASA's Kennedy Space Center on Sunday night. Their itinerary requires them to spend 27 hours inside the capsule, which they named named \"Resilience,\" before reaching the space station.</p><p>So on Monday, the crew took a few minutes to show the world their spaceship.</p><p>\"Good morning, good afternoon, good evening, and welcome onboard Crew Dragon Resilience,\" Mission Commander Mike Hopkins says in the video, which NASA <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=21X5lGlDOfg\">streamed live</a>. \"Victor, Shannon, Soichi, and I are very pleased to welcome you on board as we journey to the International Space Station.\"&#160;</p><p>You can watch their video tour below.</p><iframe width=\"560\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/TT6BC68UzeY?start=256\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe><h2>'It's actually quite nice'</h2><p>The launch of Crew-1, as the mission is called, marked the beginning of one of SpaceX's most important flights yet: the company's first full-length crewed mission for NASA. It's the company's second time launching people into space, but the longest-duration human spaceflight ever launched from the US. The current record, 84 days, has held since the longest Skylab mission more than 45 years ago.</p><p>Once the Crew Dragon docks to the ISS on Monday night, the astronauts are expected to live and work on the orbiting laboratory for about half a year.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fac65cf98669500182b5866?format=jpeg\" alt=\"crew 1 kennedy\" height=\"604\" width=\"1041\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>NASA astronauts (from left) Shannon Walker, Victor Glover and Mike Hopkins, and Japan Aerospace Exploration Agency (JAXA) astronaut Soichi Noguchi, right, speak to press at NASA&#39;s Kennedy Space Center in Cape Canaveral, Florida, Sunday, November 8, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NASA</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Hopkins began the video tour of the Crew Dragon by showing off its cockpit, where astronauts sit for launch and landing. He described the three touch display screens from which they can monitor and control the spacecraft.</p><p>\"We can bring up maps that show where we are over the Earth, and it's actually quite nice,\" he said.</p><p>Hopkins then passed the mic to Glover, the crew's rookie crew member. Glover, the mission's pilot, had logged more than 3,000 hours of flight experience on Earth but had never been to space before.&#160;With him in the video is the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/spacex-nasa-astronauts-launched-baby-yoda-doll-crew-dragon-spaceship-2020-11\">Baby Yoda stuffed toy</a> that the crew brought up to serve as an indicator that the spaceship had entered microgravity.</p><p>\"Hello everyone, Victor here,\" Glover said in the video. \"Baby Yoda and I wanted to talk to you a little bit about the hatches.\"</p><p>Floating near an entryway, he continued,&#160;\"just about 24 hours ago, we entered Resilience through this side hatch.\"</p><p>The crew won't open that hatch again until after they've safely splashed down in the Atlantic Ocean at the end of the mission. When they dock to the ISS, they will enter via the forward hatch at the top of the capsule.&#160;</p><p>During his turn with the mic, Noguchi described the capsule's storage area, and Walker then explained where the crew keeps emergency supplies and clothes. She also demonstrated how to drink from a water bottle in microgravity.&#160;</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb30361402d49001924f480?format=jpeg\" alt=\"crew 1 baby yoda shannon walker crew dragon resilience tour astronauts orbit spacex nasa mike hopkins victor glover soichi noguchi jaxa\" height=\"1619\" width=\"2160\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Baby Yoda lurks over NASA astronaut Shannon Walker&#39;s shoulder as she gives a tour of the Resilience capsule, November 16, 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">NASA TV</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The tour culminated in a heartfelt moment as the team lined up for an in-flight ceremony. Once an astronaut completes two years of basic training, Hopkins explained, they get a silver pin – the sign of an \"unflown\" astronaut. But once they've traveled 100 kilometers above the Earth, the astronaut receives a golden pin.</p><p>\"We have one member of our crew who does not have the appropriate, uh, accoutrements for his uniform,\" he said,&#160; turning to Glover.</p><p>Hopkins then passed a gold pin to Glover, who held it up to the camera.</p><p>\"Congratulations,\" he said, as Noguchi and Glover fist-bumped.&#160;</p><p>\"All for one, Crew-1 for all,\" the team said before signing off.</p><p><em>Morgan McFall-Johnsen contributed reporting.&#160;</em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the ski resorts and ski hotels will look a little different this year due to COVID-19.</li><li>However, skiing and snowboarding present an especially appealing option as a safer outdoor activity this winter.</li><li>We've rounded up the best ski hotels across the US to suit a range of price points from $175 to $597 to start.</li><li>We've also outlined each hotel's current COVID-19 policies and changes.</li><li>Are hotels safe? An infectious disease doctor, a cleaning expert, and hotel reps all share what you should know before you check-in</a>.</li></ul><p>Winter is right around the corner and snow is already falling on mountains across the country. Although ski season hasn't been canceled this year, things are going to look different than they have in the past as resorts work to create a safe environment for all their guests amidst the ongoing pandemic.</p><p>Redesigned lift lines will spread out across the snow to allow for social distancing and drinking a beer with those in your travel pod by an outdoor firepit will replace standing boot to boot in packed après ski bars. Many mountains will also require advance reservations. And if you've never been one to wear a balaclava, well, this is your year.</p><p>Still, getting into the mountains can be an appealing pandemic-friendly activity. Aside from the joy delivered by schussing down a snowy trail, ski resorts — and the hotels that serve them — offer an abundance of cold-weather outdoor adventures beyond the slopes from cross-country skiing and snowshoeing to dog sledding.&#160;</p><p>Before planning a snowy getaway, it's important to keep in mind that the pandemic continues to sweep across the US and that many states are experiencing serious spikes in cases right now. If you're wondering if it's<a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/is-travel-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> safe to travel at all</a>, we talked to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/are-hotels-safe-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">experts about the risks, as well as the best precautions to take</a>. Additionally, each hotel on this list is committed to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/hotel-precautions-coronavirus\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">rigorous new cleaning protocols</a> in an effort to mitigate the risks associated with contracting COVID-19. We outlined these measures below.</p><p>It's also vital to note that there is never a guarantee of safety when it comes to travel right now, even if you plan to spend much of your time outdoors. We recommend following CDC guidelines, and always advise travelers to wear a mask, wash hands frequently, and maintain social distancing. Additionally, consider your own level of risk, and whether you're traveling from or to a hotspot, so as not to increase the rate of infection.</p><p>You should also research individual state's travel restrictions before you book. Since the situation is constantly evolving, it's wise to read up on <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/coronavirus-hotel-airbnb-cancellation-change-policies\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">hotel cancellation policies</a> in case your plans may need to change. That said, if you're ready to hunker down in a mountain chic retreat with views of the slopes, there are plenty of ski hotel options across the US.&#160;</p><p><strong>We've carefully curated top US ski hotels based on the following criteria:</strong></p><ol><li>Nearly all of these hotels are located one-mile or less from the slopes and offer either ski-in/ski-out or a complimentary shuttle service to deliver guests to and from the mountain. For the few that are a little farther afield, they are still within an easy and short drive of the lifts.</li><li>In addition to providing guests with prime access to downhill skiing and riding, each of these properties offers abundant winter sports adventures including Nordic skiing and snowshoeing, ice skating, sleigh rides, and sledding— either on-site or very close by.</li><li>All hotels are well-appointed stays with plenty of skier-friendly amenities like ski valets, on-site spas, hot tubs, outdoor heated pools, and saunas.</li><li>Skiing can be notoriously pricey and we've kept affordability in mind. id=\"slideshow\">\n\tTrapp Family Lodge – Stowe, Vermont\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb29a701c741f0019ac9f43?format=jpeg\" alt=\"trapp family lodge\" height=\"960\" width=\"1280\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Booking.com</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=6776&#38;awinaffid=257137&#38;clickref=&#38;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fus%2Ftrapp-family-lodge.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Book Trapp Family Lodge starting at $175 per night</a></h2><p>Set on 2,500 pastoral acres just outside the classic New England village of Stowe, this charming, Austrian-style chalet has been welcoming visitors since 1950. Owned and operated by the von Trapp family, whose story has been immortalized by the beloved film \"The Sound of Music,\" the Trapp Family Lodge is home to 96 rooms and suites, 18 luxurious villas, and 100 hillside guesthouses.</p><p>Nordic skiers and snowshoe aficionados will delight in exploring the resort's extensive trail network, which includes more than 40 miles of groomed trails and an additional 60 miles of forested backcountry. Winter adventures, including horse-drawn sleigh rides, set out from Trapp's outdoor center, where you can rent equipment, sign up for lessons, or shop for cozy winter gear. Meanwhile, what may just be the East Coast's best alpine skiing and riding can be found right up the Mountain Road at Stowe Mountain Resort, home to 485-acres of terrain spread across Mount Mansfield and Spruce Peak.</p><p>Trapp's state-of-the-art fitness center, located a few steps from the Lodge, features an indoor pool and an outdoor hot tub as well as a sauna and three inviting massage rooms where you can relax with a therapeutic rubdown. Throughout the property, fireplaces glow in the Lodge's inviting public spaces while European-inspired guestrooms and suites, which offer warm, fluffy duvets, wood-beamed ceilings, and beautiful views of the surrounding mountains and hillsides.</p><p>Don't miss a stop at Brewing Bierhall just up the road for an apr&#232;s-ski hang serving up Austrian specialties and farm-to-fork Vermont fare.</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.tripadvisor.com/Hotel_Review-g57415-d100122-Reviews-Trapp_Family_Lodge-Stowe_Vermont.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Trip Advisor</a> Rating:</strong> 5 out of 25 hotels in Stowe</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=6776&#38;awinaffid=257137&#38;clickref=&#38;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fus%2Ftrapp-family-lodge.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow nofollow noopener sponsored sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Booking.com</a> Rating:</strong> 8.9 out of 10</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Trapp Family Lodge offers a range of additional activities like family history tours, maple sugaring walks, tours of the brewery, movie nights (guess which one?), and sing-a-longs. The indoor pool is fabulous for families while Trapp's Nordic center is one of the country's best.</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> There is no shuttle service to Stowe Mountain Resort, although the mountain is just eight miles from the Lodge. The Lodge also charges a $35 resort fee.</p><p><strong>COVID status and policies</strong>: This hotel is open with new policies including:</p><ul><li>All guests will complete a health questionnaire prior to checking in and there is a designated health officer on-site at every shift.</li><li>&#160;All employees will complete training on mandatory health and safety requirements as provided by Vermont OSHA.</li><li>&#160;Housekeeping daily service and turndown service has been suspended but are available by request.</li><li>&#160;Guest tours and activities will comply with gathering sizes and physical distancing.</li><li>&#160;All common spaces and high-touch surfaces will be cleaned regularly, in accordance with CDC guidance.</li></ul>\n\tOmni Mount Washington Resort – Bretton Woods, New Hampshire\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5fb29d321c741f0019ac9f58?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Omni Mount Washington Resort \" height=\"854\" width=\"1138\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Trip Advisor</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h2><a href=\"https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=6776&#38;awinaffid=257137&#38;clickref=&#38;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.booking.com%2Fhotel%2Fus%2Fomni-mount-washington-resort.en-gb.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Book Omni Mount Washington Resort starting at $179 per night</a></h2><p>Commissioned by wealthy New Hampshire Industrialist Joseph Stickney and built by over 250 Italian craftsmen, the majestic Omni Mount Washington Resort first opened its doors in 1902 to a stream of high society summer travelers from Boston, New York, and Philadelphia. And though this grand property in the heart of the White Mountains has been delivering elegant New England hospitality to its guests for more than a century, 1999 marked the resort's first winter season.</p><p>These days, it's hard to imagine that the hotel hasn't always been courting cold-season guests. The hotel enjoys a prime location barely a mile from Bretton Woods Ski Area, which at 464-acres, is New Hampshire's largest ski resort.</p><p>Inside you'll find the hotel's opulent Great Hall, complete with huge chandeliers, a massive stone fireplace, and an antique grandfather clock that has kept time in the lobby since the hotel's earliest days. Guestrooms and suites run the gamut from snug, queen-bedded European Rooms to king and corner rooms with views of snow-covered mountains and spacious family suites. In 1969, Robert Redford bought the land now known as Sundance with the mission \"to develop a little and preserve a great deal.\" The result? A vibrant arts and recreational community nestled at the base of the majestic Mount Timpanogos where visitors relish the resort's wintry beauty and vintage mountain charm.</p><p>If you've ever drooled over the gorgeous wares in the Sundance catalog, you'll love the way that same vibrant, artistic flair influences the entire resort. Natural wood, leather, and stone feature prominently throughout the warm, colorful space. Native American art and the work of local craftspeople complete the nature-focused vibe. The hotel includes 96 guestrooms and suites and 10 private mountain homes that are clustered throughout the property and include everything from cozy, standard rooms that sleep two to romantic suites and spacious lofts. Get the lay of the land with a guided mountain tour before hitting the trails on your own. Steep bowls showcase Utah's epic powder and for some real old-school fun, the resort keeps the bulk of the front mountain open for night skiing four nights a week.</p><p>Apr&#232;s ski, pop into the historic Owl Bar for cocktails and poutine, Transplanted from Thermopolis, Wyoming, the bar was once the favorite watering hole of Butch Cassidy and his Hole in the Wall Gang.&#160;</p><p><strong><a href=\"https://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/6415797/type/dlg/https://www.tripadvisor.com/Hotel_Review-g57140-d116058-Reviews-Sundance_Resort-Sundance_Utah.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Trip Advisor</a> Ranking:</strong> 1 out of 1 hotel in Sundance</p><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Sundance's slopes are right outside your door and two lift tickets are included with every room. The Inn, which features 142 rooms and suites, a gorgeous, LEED-certified spa, and endless winter activities, offers a blend of traditional New England charm and sleek modern touches.</p><p>Guests looking for that quintessential, Vermont ski experience can take the Inn's shuttle to nearby Suicide Six, one of the oldest ski areas in the US and home to the country's first rope tow. Right in the heart of Teton Village just steps from the mountain, the boutique Hotel Terra is Wyoming's first LEED Silver-certified property and features cowboy-chic decor with a sleek, eco-friendly twist. Guestrooms have heated floors, organic mattresses and linens, aluminum bath dispensers, and energy-efficient lighting.</p><p>Hotel Terra's 132 stylish guestrooms range from traditional rooms and studio-style abodes to spacious two and three-bedroom suites. Jackson Hole sees almost 500-inches of champagne powder every year and conditions border on sublime. Hop on the mountain's Aerial Tram (or, as locals call it \"the red heli,\" \"the box,\" or \"big red\") to Rendezvous Peak. Look down as you near the summit for a bird's-eye view of Corbet's Couloir, one of the toughest runs out there. From the tram, dip into Rendezvous Bowl, a massive, open field that spills into the smaller Cheyenne Bowl below.</p><p>Reward a day on the mountain with one of the many nature-inspired treatments offered at the rooftop Chill Spa where the signature Herbal Poultice Massage uses a steamed infusion of ginger, turmeric, and lemongrass works tired bodies into a puddle of bliss. With 3,460 feet of vertical, Whiteface boasts the steepest drop this side of the Rockies. Expert skiers will love The Slides, a series of narrow, double black diamond chutes that plunge into the wilderness. But you don't have to be an Olympian to enjoy the rest of the mountain's terrain and there are plenty of blue square trails to enjoy too. Don't miss the 2.1-mile Wilmington Trail, which treats skiers and riders to the longest intermediate run in the northeast and gorgeous views of the surrounding Adirondack Mountains.</p><p>Back at the Lodge, guests will delight in architectural details reminiscent of the Great Camps of a bygone era thanks to warm paneling covering the walls, rustic handcrafted furniture, and huge fieldstone fireplaces that invite lingering. Guest accommodations include five Main Lodge rooms, 17 shoreline cabins, six stunning Lakeside Building suites, and two private cottages. Every room has its own unique, Adirondack charm and features plush bedding, a wood-burning fireplace, and gorgeous views of the lake and snowy woodlands through diamond-pane windows.</p><p>The landscape surrounding the Lodge is truly a winter wonderland with trails for snowshoeing and Nordic skiing right outside the door and a host of activities nearby, including dogsledding, ice skating, and toboggan rides on Mirror Lake. 51-026_2667d293c22f2702.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn83@2020_3/2020/11/17/05-38-53-238_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=LgpNjolxaes:-qBslcaeALw:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn72@2020_4/2020/11/17/05-38-48-071_b7bfe306f4f377a7.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/LgpNjolxaes":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn39@2020_5/2020/11/17/05-39-02-257_4aafb0c54b5bdfba.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1605591522192},{"createdTime":"2020-11-17 </img>\n</figure>\n<ul class=\"summary-list\"> \n <li>The majority of counties in the state of California have moved to the \"purple tier\" denotation — the most serious of the state's ranking system.&nbsp;</li> \n <li>Under the purple designation, \"many\" non-essential businesses are forced to halt their indoor operations to stem the spread of the novel coronavirus.</li> \n <li>California over the weekend became the second state to report more than 1 million COVID-19 cases, joining Texas.&nbsp;</li> \n <li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li> \n</ul>\n<p>The majority - 41 of 58 —of counties in the state of California were <a href=\"https://twitter.com/GavinNewsom/status/1328447741341560833\">classified by state officials Monday</a> in the purple tier, the state's designation for areas hardest hit by COVID-19 infections. The move comes days after California <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/california-the-second-state-to-pass-1-million-covid-19-cases-1029800981\">surpassed one million confirmed cases of the virus</a>, a metric so far only matched by the state of Texas.</p>\n<p>The California designation includes the state's most populous regions, including the counties of Los Angeles, San Diego, Orange, Riverside, and San Bernardino.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>According to California's \"<a href=\"https://covid19.ca.gov/safer-economy/\">Blueprint for a Safer Economy</a>,\" \"many\" non-essential businesses must cease indoor operations when counties are moved to the purple tier. Counties move into the purple when they have an adjusted case rate greater than seven and a positivity rate greater than 8%.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Other tiers include red, where \"some\" indoor businesses are required to close, the orange tier, where \"some\" indoor businesses can remain open but with modifications, and the yellow tier, where the majority of businesses are open with normal operations, according to <a href=\"https://covid19.ca.gov/safer-economy/\">the state guidelines</a>.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Also Monday, <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ZavalaA/status/1328436236436926464\">Newsom told reporters he was \"considering\" implementing a statewide curfew</a>, though he said a final decision had not been reached. New York Gov. Over the past week, 4.8% of COVID-19 tests in the state have returned a positive result, about half of the 9.8% national positivity rate, according to the data.</p>\n<p>There have been at least 13:38:42","updatedTime":"2020-11-17 13:38:42","title":"7 easy ways to speed up your Windows 10 computer, from disabling unneeded effects to upgrading your hardware","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-speed-up-windows-10","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f120f403ad861532d37e3d4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Laptops 1\" height=\"1125\" width=\"2250\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>It&#39;s easy to speed up a Windows 10 computer, no matter how old it is.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Hollis Johnson</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>To speed up your Windows 10 computer, you should uninstall programs you don't want, turn off special effects, and change your startup settings.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>The single most effective way to speed up Windows 10, however, is to use a Solid State Drive.</strong></li>\n<li><strong>You should also make sure Windows 10 is up-to-date, and that your computer is running at full power.</strong></li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\">Visit Business Insider's Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p>People sometimes wonder how it was possible for the guidance computer in Apollo 11 — a computer with less memory than the cheapest <a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=bi_080719_speed-up-windows-10&u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fwindows-10-home-english-windows%2F6121415.p%3FskuId%3D61214151415\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Windows 10</a>&#160;PC in use today — to reach the moon.&#160;</p><p>The answer: It didn't waste any processing power on a fancy interface, or multi-tasking.&#160;</p><p>You can eke some extra performance out of your own Windows 10 computer by making it a little more minimalist, like that original Apollo 11 computer. You can also give it a straight upgrade.</p><p>Here are seven ways you can speed up your Windows 10 computer right now.&#160;</p>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tReduce the amount of apps that open at startup\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41aa0048c50a1a95519be1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows speed 1\" height=\"1292\" width=\"1435\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can disable slow startup programs in the Task Manager.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>If your computer takes a long time to boot, the most likely culprit is that you have too many programs slowing down the startup process.&#160;</p><p>This means there may be a lot of unnecessary programs running in the background, which continue to slow things down even after Windows is fully booted. Here's how to fix it:</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Right-click the Start button and choose \"Task Manager.\"</p><p><strong>2. </strong>In Task Manager, click the \"Startup\" tab.</p><p><strong>3. </strong>If you see a program you don't want to run at startup, right-click it and choose \"Disable.\"</p>\n\tUninstall bloatware and other unwanted programs\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41aa99100a2431ad4043d4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows 10 office man computer\" height=\"1496\" width=\"1994\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Windows computers come preloaded with tons of proprietary software.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Shutterstock</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>There's a good chance your computer came with a number of unwanted programs that run in the background and slow things down. Often called \"bloatware,\" they rarely serve a useful purpose.&#160;</p><p>You should take a few minutes to uninstall programs you don't want or need from your computer.</p><p>To do that, follow the steps in <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-uninstall-programs-on-windows-10\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">our article on how to properly uninstall programs on Windows 10</a>.</p>\n\tDisable Windows special effects\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41ab3c100a242a3a05cf37?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows speed\" height=\"1494\" width=\"1982\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can disable special effects to improve your computer&#39;s performance.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Windows 10 has a lot of special effects &#8212; some very obvious, others quite subtle. They make the experience of using your computer more fun and enjoyable, but they might also be slowing your PC down, especially if it's older or has a slow processor.&#160;</p><p>Here's how to turn off some of these special effects.</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Click the Start button and start the Control Panel.&#160;</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Click \"System.\"</p><p><strong>3. </strong>Click \"Advanced system settings.\"</p><p><strong>4. </strong>On the System Properties window, make sure you are on the Advanced tab and click \"Settings.\"</p><p><strong>5. </strong>Here you can manually turn off special effects or just click \"Adjust for best performance.\"</p>\n\tTurn off window transparency\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41ab54100a2466fc6d7385?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows speed 3\" height=\"1452\" width=\"1756\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The transparency effect is so subtle you might not notice it’s been turned off.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>You might not have noticed, but there are some subtle transparency effects built into Windows. Open the Start menu, for example, and you should see a faint, blurred impression of whatever lies behind it.&#160;</p><p>If you don't want to sacrifice processing speed for such a small effect, you can turn it off entirely (and probably not notice the aesthetic difference).&#160;</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Click the Start button and click the Settings icon, which is shaped like a gear and is right above the Power icon.&#160;</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Click \"Personalization.\"</p><p><strong>3. </strong>Click \"Colors.\"</p><p><strong>4. </strong>Scroll down and turn off \"Transparency effects\" by sliding the switch to the left.</p>\n\tRun your computer at full power\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41aba0100a24166314f8ed?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows speed 4\" height=\"919\" width=\"1838\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Unless you often use your laptop on battery power without a charger, you can probably choose the &#34;high performance&#34; power plan.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Your computer might be running at less than full speed, depending upon how your power management controls are set.&#160;</p><p>Designed to make your laptop battery last longer, Windows offers several power plans that deliberately slow down your PC to save power. Here's how to choose a higher power plan:</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Click the Start button and start the Control Panel.&#160;</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Click \"Power Options.\"</p><p><strong>3. </strong>For the best overall processing speed, choose \"High performance.\"&#160;</p><p>If you're not on a laptop, you probably won't see these options.</p>\n\tKeep Windows up to date\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41abec100a2416a2082af3?format=jpeg\" alt=\"windows speed 5\" height=\"1305\" width=\"1740\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Make sure your computer is up to date for the best performance.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Dave Johnson/Business Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Make sure your computer stays up to date. Microsoft issues regular patches and updates for Windows, and while many of these are related to improving your computer's security (which is also important), some also improve performance.&#160;</p><p>To see if there are updates waiting to be installed:</p><p><strong>1. </strong>Click the Start button and click the Settings icon, which is shaped like a gear and is right above the Power icon.&#160;</p><p><strong>2. </strong>Click \"Update &#38; security.\"</p><p><strong>3. </strong>You can check for updates or install and updates waiting to be installed.&#160;</p>\n\tUse an SSD or install additional memory\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5d41ac93100a24307600fa75?format=jpeg\" alt=\"WD solid state drive\" height=\"519\" width=\"550\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Installing a solid-state drive into your computer will give its performance a boost.\n<p class=\"copyright\">WD</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p>Finally, you can dramatically improve the performance of your computer by increasing its memory and storage.&#160;</p><p>If your computer has a traditional hard drive &#8212; one with spinning metal platters &#8212; replacing it with a <a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=bi_080719_speed-up-windows-10-ssd&#38;u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fsandisk-ultra-512gb-internal-sata-solid-state-drive%2F5969506.p%3FskuId%3D5969506%26ref%3D199%26loc%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo%26acampID%3D1%26siteID%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo-l96q5A0mmVB9UIaI8l0XtQ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">solid-state drive (SSD)</a> can make a world of difference. An <a href=\"http://bestbuy.7tiv.net/c/196318/614286/10014?subId1=bi_080719_speed-up-windows-10-ssd&#38;u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bestbuy.com%2Fsite%2Fsandisk-ultra-512gb-internal-sata-solid-state-drive%2F5969506.p%3FskuId%3D5969506%26ref%3D199%26loc%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo%26acampID%3D1%26siteID%3DEHFxW6yx8Uo-l96q5A0mmVB9UIaI8l0XtQ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">SSD</a> has the same kind of memory as a USB flash drive (though much, much faster) and it'll allow Windows to boot several times faster, and programs to start in a fraction of the time.&#160;</p><p>Adding an SSD is the single biggest improvement you can make to a PC, and it can even make a bigger difference than upgrading to a computer with a faster processor.&#160;</p><p>In addition, if you use your computer for a lot of resource-intensive tasks, like photo editing, video production, or gaming, adding additional memory can help as well.</p><p>You should have no less than 4GB of RAM in your computer for Windows to run efficiently, but adding additional memory can improve performance.&#160;</p><section data-track-content=\"\"
