Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>As the nation's coronavirus case count climbs, the White House continues to grapple with its own string of outbreaks.</p><p>More than two dozen high-profile officials associated with President Donald Trump have contracted COVID-19 since the start of the pandemic. Trump and his allies have <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/photos-trump-before-his-positive-covid-19-test-maskless-near-people-2020-10\">regularly dismissed</a> Centers for Disease Control and Prevention recommendations, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-told-woodward-he-always-downplayed-threat-of-covid-19-2020-9\">downplayed</a> the severity of the virus, and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/donald-trump-coronavirus-infections-records-health-campaign-election-2020-10\">disputed</a> the immense criticism they've received over the past several months. The disease has spread through the president's orbit, infecting White House staffers, campaign aides, and Republican leaders — including <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-coronavirus-treatments-prognosis-puzzle-doctors-remdesivir-dexamethasone-2020-10\">Trump himself</a>.</p><p>At least eight of the confirmed cases have been linked to a White House ceremony <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/everyone-attended-supreme-court-pick-event-tested-covid-19-positive-2020-10\">on September 26</a>, when over 150 people — closely seated and many maskless — gathered in the White House's Rose Garden for then Judge Amy Coney Barrett's Supreme Court nomination. Public-health officials, including the nation's top infectious-disease expert, Dr. Anthony Fauci, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/fauci-white-house-outbreak-coronavirus-superspreader-event-2020-10\">later dubbed</a> the event a superspreader.</p><p>Former New Jersey Gov. Chris Christie, a Republican ally to Trump who attended the announcement and afterward battled the disease for a week in the intensive-care unit, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/chris-christie-wrong-not-to-wear-mask-white-house-2020-10\">expressed regret</a> over his choice to ignore public-health guidelines. \"I was wrong,\" he said.</p><p>Trump also tested positive for the coronavirus after the gathering and was <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-walter-reed-medical-center-hospital-covid-fever-cough-19-2020-10\">hospitalized</a> for three nights at Walter Reed National Military Medical Center, where he was treated with experimental drugs. After his release and recovery, he <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-downplays-covid-19-while-announcing-hell-leave-hospital-2020-10\">continued to</a> undermine the virus' threat.&#160;</p><p>Another recent explosion of cases has been connected to an election-night party hosted at the White House. Several in attendance, including White House chief of staff Mark Meadows, Housing and Urban Development Secretary Ben Carson, Republican National Committee staffers, and campaign advisors, later tested positive.</p><p>This chart shows all the people with confirmed cases and their relationships to the president.</p><div class=\"insider-raw-embed\"><div id=graphic-embed></div><script Tesla logo is seen on a car in Los Angeles, California, U.S., July 9, 2020.  REUTERS/Lucy Nicholson     TPX IMAGES OF THE DAY\" height=\"2206\" width=\"3309\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Shares of Tesla spiked by more than 13% on the news.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Tesla will join the S&#38;P 500 on December 21, S&#38;P Dow Jones Indices announced Monday</li>\n<li>With a market cap of nearly $400 billion, Tesla is set to join as one of the 10 most valuable companies in the index.&#160;</li>\n<li>S&#38;P Global did not say which company Tesla will replace later this year.&#160;</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Tesla will be added to the S&#38;P 500 later this year, S&#38;P Dow Jones Indices <a href=\"https://www.spglobal.com/spdji/en/media-center/news-announcements/#indexNews\">announced</a> Monday.&#160;</p><p>Tesla will join the exclusive club of companies prior to the open of trading on Monday, December 21. <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/tsla-stock\">Shares of the electric-vehicle manufacturer</a> jumped more than 13% on the news in after-hours trading.&#160;</p><p>The S&#38;P 500, an index of 500 large US companies, is seen as one of the most important gauges of the success of America's largest publicly-traded firms. It is chosen by the S&#38;P 500 Index Committee, which rebalances the group each quarter. In September, the online marketplace Etsy, robotics company Teradyne, and pharmaceutical developer Catalent joined the index, while Tesla was left out, even though it met the standards required to be added.&#160;</p><p>Among other <a href=\"https://www.spglobal.com/spdji/en/documents/additional-material/sp-500-brochure.pdf\">requirements</a>, companies must be based in the US, have a market cap of at least $8.2 billion, be highly liquid, have at least 50% of their shares available to the public, and post four consecutive profitable quarters, a <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/tesla-stock-price-reaction-4th-quarterly-profit-sp500-elon-musk-2020-7-1029423950\">criterion Tesla met</a> in the period ending June 30.&#160;</p><p>Tesla joins the index as the world's most valuable automaker, with a market cap of nearly $400 billion. That places it firmly in the top 10 most valuable firms in the index, alongside Goliaths like Apple, Amazon, and Berkshire Hathaway.&#160;</p><p><em><strong>Read More:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-to-buy-polestar-2-electric-car-ev-volvo-dealership-2020-9?r=tl-sub\">Polestar's business model centers on what many flashy EV startups lack: a robust service network from Volvo</a></em></p><p>Even as the pandemic dealt a major blow to the global auto industry, disrupting manufacturing and supply chains worldwide, Tesla has had one of its best years to date. Last month, the EV maker <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-earnings-q3-2020-third-quarter-profit-2020-10\">reported its fifth straight profitable quarter</a>. Tesla also said in October it <a href=\"https://ir.tesla.com/press-release/tesla-q3-2020-vehicle-production-deliveries\">sold 139,300</a> cars from July through September, beating its previous quarterly sales record by more than 20,000 vehicles and putting it within spitting distance of its goal to sell 500,000 cars in 2020. Shares of Tesla have more than quadrupled this year.</p><p>S&#38;P Global did not specify which of the current 500 firms Tesla would replace, saying that it would make that announcement in a separate release.&#160;</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-to-join-sp-500-in-december-2020-11'>Business Insider</a></div><div
